<div class="lead    dark-bg-copy ">
    <p style="text-align: center;">The AWS Cloud operates 44 Availability Zones within 16 geographic  Regions around the world, with announced plans for 17 more Availability  Zones and six more Regions in Bahrain, China, France, Hong Kong, Sweden,  and a second AWS GovCloud Region in the US.<br />
</p>

</div>
